124a3(nyi khri): mnga'o/ /dgongs pa yongs su nyams pa mi mnga'o/ /ting nge 'dzin yongs su nyams pa mi mnga'o/ /shes rab yongs su nyams pa mi mnga'o/ /rnam par grol ba yongs su nyams pa mi mnga'o/ /rnam par grol ba'i ye shes
124a4(nyi khri): gzigs pa yongs su nyams pa mi mnga'o/ /sku'i phrin las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ste/ ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ngo / /gsung gi phrin las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ste/ ye shes kyi rjes su
124a5(nyi khri): 'brang ngo / /thugs kyi phrin las thams cad ye shes sngon du 'gro ba ste/ ye shes kyi rjes su 'brang ngo / /'das pa'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes gzigs pa 'jug go/ /ma 'ongs pa'i dus la ma chags
124a6(nyi khri): ma thogs pa'i ye shes gzigs pa 'jug go/ /da ltar byung ba'i dus la ma chags ma thogs pa'i ye shes gzigs pa 'jug ste/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa rnams so/ /rab 'byor de bzhin
124a7(nyi khri): gshegs pa'i rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid gang zhe na/ gang la dmigs pa med pa/ dran pas dbang bsgyur ba/ zhi ba'i rnam pa dang ldan pa'i mtshan nyid med pa'i mtshan nyid ni rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid ces bya'o/ /
124a8(nyi khri): shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa stong phrag nyi shu lnga pa/ bam po drug bcu brgyad pa/ de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mi chen po'i mtshan sum bcu rtsa gnyis gang zhe na/ phyag dang zhabs 'khor
124b1(nyi khri): lo'i mtshan dang ldan pa dang / zhabs shin tu gnas pa dang / phyag dang zhabs dra bar 'brel pa dang / phyag dang zhabs gzhon zhing 'jam pa dang / bdun shin du mtho ba dang / sor mo ring ba dang / rting pa yangs pa dang / sku che
124b2(nyi khri): zhing drang ba dang / zhabs legs par mtho ba dang / yan lag gi spu gyen du 'khyil ba dang / ri dgas e na ya'i byin pa lta bu dang / phyag brla drang por slebs pa dang / gsang ba'i gnas sbubs su nub pa dang /
124b3(nyi khri): gser gyi kha dog dang / mdog shin tu 'jam pa dang / spu re re nas g.yas phyogs su 'khyil ba dang / zhal mdzod spus brgyan pa dang / seng ge'i ro stod lta bu dang / phrag pa'i lhun mdzes par grub pa dang /
124b4(nyi khri): phrag so shin tu rgyas pa dang / ro bro ba'i mchog dang / shing n+ya gro da ltar chu zheng gab pa dang / dbu spyi gtsug dang ldan pa dang / ljags shin du yangs pa dang / tshangs pa'i dbyangs dang / seng ge'i 'gram
124b5(nyi khri): pa lta bu dang / tshems shin tu dkar ba dang / tshems shin tu mnyam pa dang / tshems thags bzang ba dang / tshems mnyam zhing bzhi bcu tshang ba dang / spyan dkar nag 'byes pa dang / ba'i rdzi ma lta bu ste/
124b6(nyi khri): de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag dang zhabs kyi mthil la 'khor lo rtsibs stong dang ldan pa mu khyud can lte ba dang bcas pa/ rnam pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa 'di lta ste/ rus pa 'am ba so la gzugs
124b7(nyi khri): brkos pa dang 'dra ba mnga' bas/ phyag dang zhabs 'khor lo'i mtshan dang ldan pa'o/ /zhabs kyi mthil gnyis mnyam par sa la 'jog cing zhabs zhum pa med pas zhabs shin tu gnas pa'o/ /
124b8(nyi khri): ngang pa'i rgyal po ltar phyag dang zhabs kyi sor mo dra bar 'brel bas/ phyag dang zhabs dra bar 'brel pa'o/ /shing bal gyi sgo nga ltar shin du 'jam zhing gzhon pas phyag dang zhabs gzhon zhing 'jam pa'o/ /phyag dang
125a1(nyi khri): zhabs dang mgur gyi lhun shin du mtho bas bdun shin du mtho ba'o/ /phyag dang zhabs kyi sor mo ring bas sor mo ring ba'o/ /rting pa ring bas rting pa yangs pa'o/ /sku lag pa mdun du
125a2(nyi khri): 'phags la drang bas sku che zhing drang ba'o/ /pus mo'i lha nga dang long bu mdzes par nub pas zhabs legs par mtho ba'o/ /spu gyen du g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pas yan lag gi spu gyen du 'khyil pa'o/ /
125a3(nyi khri): ri dgas e ne ya'i byin pa dang / smig ma dang / ldum bu ngar ba ltar drang zhing ma nyams la/ rim gyis gzhol bar grub cing / byin pa zlum pas ri dgas e ne ya'i byin pa lta bu'o/ /brla drang por bzhag ste ma btud
125a4(nyi khri): kyang phyag gi mthil gnyis kyis pus mo'i lha nga la reg pas phyag brla drang por slebs pa'o/ /glang po dang rta cang shes ltar gsang ba'i gnas shin du mdzes par sbubs su nub pas/ gsang ba'i gnas
125a5(nyi khri): sbubs su nub pa'o/ /shin du sbyangs pa'i gser gyi kha dog lta bu dang ldan pas gser gyi kha dog go/ /gser dang dngul shin du sbyangs pa ltar 'jam zhing snyoms pa'i mdog tu 'dug la sku
125a6(nyi khri): la rdul gyis mi gos pas mdog shin du 'jam pa'o/ /shin du rnam par phye ba'i spu re rer skyes shing gnyis su med pas/ spu re re nas g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pa'o/ /me tog kun da dang / zla ba dang /
125a7(nyi khri): 'o ma dang / ba mo'i mdog ltar 'dug la/ nyi ma dang zla ba brgya las kyang 'phags par 'od gsal ba'i mdzod spus smin mtshams shin du brgyan pas zhal mdzod spus brgyan pa'o/ /ro stod che bas seng
125a8(nyi khri): ge'i ro stod do/ /mgur dang rgyud legs par 'brel cing / lhun zlum pas phrag pa'i lhun mdzes par grub pa'o/ /gser gyi gtan pa shin du phyis pa ltar phrag so legs par grub pas phrag so shin
125b1(nyi khri): du rgyas pa'o/ /rlung dang mkhris pa dang / bad kan gyis ma nyams shing / rnam par shes pa 'dra ba med pas ro bro ba'i mchog go/ /sku chu zheng 'dom du mnyam pas shing nya gro da ltar chu zheng
125b2(nyi khri): gab pa'o/ /spyi gtsug zlum zhing legs la g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pa dang ldan pas dbu mnyam zhing legs par grub la mdzes pa mnga' bas dbu spyi gtsug dang ldan pa'o/ /me tog
125b3(nyi khri): ud pa la dmar po'i 'dab ma'i kha dog ltar 'dug cing shin du yangs pas ljags shin du yangs shing srab pa'o/ /tshangs pa dang bya ka la ping ka lta bu'i gsung mnga' bas tshangs pa'i dbyangs so/ /
125b4(nyi khri): 'gram pa me long gi dkyil 'khor ltar legs par grub cing mdzes par skyes te/ yid du 'ong bas seng ge'i 'gram pa lta bu'o/ /me tog kun da dang dung gi bcag 'phro ltar shin du dkar ba'i
125b5(nyi khri): tshems mnga' bas tshems shin du dkar ba'o/ /tshems la mtho dman med pas tshems mnyam pa'o/ /tshems la mtshams ma dod pas tshems thags bzang ba'o/ /bla 'og gye gu med pas tshems
125b6(nyi khri): mnyam zhing bzhi bcu tshang ba'o/ /dkar gnag gi cha ma 'dres la shin du rnam par dag cing mdog dmar pos ma yog pas spyan dkar nag 'byes pa'o/ /rdzi ma bla 'og shin du legs par gnas la ma 'dzing
125b7(nyi khri): bas ba'i rdzi ma lta bu'o/ /de la bla ma la bsu bskyal dang chos nyan pa la sdod pa dang / gtsug lag khang dang / mchod rten la sogs pa la bsti stang byas pas phyag dang zhabs 'khor lo'i mtshan dang
125b8(nyi khri): ldan pa ste/ de ni 'khor shin du mang ba'i snga ltas so/ /yi dam la brtan pas zhabs shin du gnas pa ste/ de ni mi g.yo zhing shin du brtan pa'i snga ltas so/ /sbyin pa dang ngag snyan pa dang / don spyod pa dang / don 'thun pa'i
126a1(nyi khri): bsdu ba rnam bzhi goms par byas pas/ phyag dang zhabs dra bas 'brel ba ste/ de ni myur du 'du ba'i snga ltas so/ /bza' ba dang / bca' ba dang / btung ba zhim zhing nyams su bde ba byin
126a2(nyi khri): pas/ phyag dang zhabs gzhon zhing 'jam pa dang / bdun shin du mtho ba ste/ de gnyis ni bza' ba dang / bca' ba dang / btung ba zhim zhing nyams su bde ba 'thob pa'i snga ltas so/ /bcings pa bkrol ba dang
126a3(nyi khri): srog gi rim gro byas pa dang / srog gcod pa spangs pas sor mo ring ba dang / rting pa yangs pa dang / sku che zhing drang ba ste/ de ni sku tshe ring ba'i snga ltas so/ /dge ba'i chos yang dag par blangs pa dang / bzung ba
126a4(nyi khri): mngon par spel cing 'grib par ma byas pas/ zhabs kyi gong mtho ba dang / yan lag gi spu gyen du 'khyil pa ste/ de ni mi nyams pa'i chos dang ldan pa'i snga ltas so/ /rig pa dang bzo'i gnas rim gror byas shing /
126a5(nyi khri): gzhan byin pa dang / bdag gis blangs pas ri dgas e na ya'i byin pa lta bu ste/ de ni myur du 'dzin pa'i snga ltas so/ /bdog cing yod pa'i nor la bslangs na mi 'gong par gtong zhing / med ces ma byas pas phyag
126a6(nyi khri): brla drang por slebs pa ste/ de ni yo byad la mnga' ba dang dul ba'i snga ltas so/ /'grogs pa dang mdza' bshes dang / gnyen pa ma phye ba dang / bye bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams tshangs pa'i spyod pa la yang dag par
126a7(nyi khri): bskul ba dang / gsang ba'i tshig yongs su bsrungs pas/ gsang ba'i gnas sbubs su nub pa ste/ de ni bu mang ba'i snga ltas so/ /stan dang gos dang khang pa dang gzhal med khang dang / gnas bzang po byin pas
126a8(nyi khri): gser gyi kha dog dang mdog shin du 'jam pa ste/ de gnyis ni gdan dang / na bza' dang / khang pa dang / gzhal med khang dang / gnas bzang po 'thob pa'i snga ltas so/ /'du 'dzi spangs pa dang / mkhan po dang / slob dpon dang /
126b1(nyi khri): pha ma dang / phu nu la sogs pa bla ma rnams la tshul dang 'dra bar rim gro byas pa dang / btsun par byas pa dang / bcol ba rnal ma gzan pas spu re re nas g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pa dang / zhal mdzod spus brgyan pa ste/ de ni

126b3(nyi khri): med pa'i snga ltas so/ /na ba rnams la rtsi dang rim gro dang sman pa dang / nyams su phan pa'i zas byin pa dang / rim gro byas pas phrag so shin du rgyas pa dang / ro bro ba'i mchog ste/ de ni nad 'ung ba'i snga
126b4(nyi khri): ltas so/ /skyed mos tshal dang / 'khor dang / btung ba dang rdzing bu dang / rgal dka' ba'i zam pa dang / kha zas dang / phreng ba'i gnas dang / stegs dang / gtsug lag khang bya ba la sogs pa gzhan mos par bya ba
126b5(nyi khri): sngon du gtong zhing / bdag gis gzhan la byin pas/ shing nya gro da ltar chu zheng gab pa dang / dbu spyi gtsug dang ldan pa ste/ de ni mnga' chen po mnga' ba'i snga ltas so/ /yun ring por tshig snyan cing 'jam pa dang / nyams su bde
126b6(nyi khri): bar smras pas/ ljags shin du yangs shing srab pa dang / tshangs pa'i dbyangs te/ de gnyis ni yan lag lnga dang ldan pa'i gsung mnga' ba'i snga ltas so/ /gsung yan lag lnga dang ldan pa zhes bya ba ni yongs su shes shing /
126b7(nyi khri): rnam par shes par 'gyur ba dang / mnyan na dga' zhing mi 'thun pa med pa dang / zab cing dbyangs rjes su 'byung ba dang / gtang mi bra zhing rnar snyan pa dang / ma 'khrugs shing gsal ba'o/ /yun ring po nas tshig kyal pa spangs
126b8(nyi khri): shing / dus su smra smra bas seng ge'i 'gram pa lta bu ste/ de ni tshig kun kyis mnyan pa'i snga ltas so/ /rim gror bya ba dang / brnyas pa med pa gnyis kyis 'tsho ba yongs su dag pas/ tshems shin du dkar ba dang mnyam pa ste/ de ni
127a1(nyi khri): 'khor snga nas bsags pa'i snga ltas so/ /yun ring po nas bden zhing phra ma med pa'i tshig smra smra bas/ tshems thags bzang ba dang / tshems mnyam zhing bzhi bcu tshang ba ste/ de ni 'khor dbyer
127a2(nyi khri): mi phyed pa'i snga ltas so/ /pang gis 'khyud pa bzhin du nyes par bsam pa med la ma chags mi sdang ba dang / rmongs pa med pa'i mig gis lta lta bas spyan dkar nag 'byes pa dang / ba'i rdzi ma lta bu ste/

128b8(nyi khri): ba ste/ ljags shin du dmar ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni glang po'i sgra dang / 'brug gi sgra lta bus bsnyengs pa mi mnga' ba ste/ glang po'i nga ro dang / 'brug gi dbyangs dang ldan pa yin/
129a1(nyi khri): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni snyan cing 'jam pa dang / nyams su bde bar smra ba'i slob ma mnga' ba ste/ snyan cing 'jam pa dang nyams su bde ba'i gsung dang ldan pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom

129a4(nyi khri): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rim gyis mngon par rtogs pa'i chos ston pa ste/ tshems mche ba rim gyis gzhol ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni shes rab kyi ri bo mthon po la bzhugs pa ste/

129a6(nyi khri): du yangs pa mnga' ba ste/ spyan ring ba dang ldan pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzigs pa shin du rnam par dag pa ste/ spyan rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi tshogs shin du

270b3(nyi khri): gshegs pa khyod kyi ston pa yin te/ khyod kyis yongs su spyad do/ /kun dga' bo khyod kyis byams pa'i lus kyi las yid du 'ong zhing / yid du mi 'ong ba ma yin pa dang / byams pa'i ngag gi las yid du 'ong zhing yid

270b5(nyi khri): pa dang dga' ba dang / bla mar byas pa de/ nga 'das pa'i 'og tu khyod kyis shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa 'di la gyis shig /kun dga' bo khyod la lan gnyis lan gsum du gtad cing rjes su gtad kyis/ khyod kyis ci nas
270b6(nyi khri): kyang shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa 'di med par mi 'gyur bar gyis shig / kun dga' bo ji srid du shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa 'di 'jig rten na gnas pa de srid du de bzhin gshegs pa yang bzhugs par rig

270b8(nyi khri): pa dang / sgrogs pa dang / ston pa dang / kha ton byed pa dang / 'dri ba dang / rim gror byed pa dang / bla mar byed pa dang / sti stang du byed pa dang / mchod par byed pa dang / rjed par byed pa dang / gus par byed cing / me tog dang / bdug pa dang / spos dang /
